# Soviet Events

add_namespace = russia2_russia

# Check if File is Loaded
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.2092066524

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = russia_reworked_events_loaded_soviets
	}
}

# Communist government in FROM baltic country and they wish to be annexed
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.4
	title = russia2_russia.4.t
	desc = russia2_russia.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_in_riga

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.4.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						tag = LIT
					}
				}
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
						target = LIT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = russia2_russia.4_threat_LIT }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						tag = FIN
					}
				}
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
						target = FIN
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					add_named_threat = { threat = 5 name = russia2_russia.4_threat_FIN }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						tag = EST
					}
				}
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
						target = EST
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = russia2_russia.4_threat_EST }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						tag = LAT
					}
				}
			 	SOV = {
			 		annex_country = {
						target = LAT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = russia2_russia.4_threat_LAT }
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {

			 FROM = {
			 	country_event = { id = russia2_baltic.6 hours = 6}
			 }
			 news_event = { id = news.69 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.4.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

# Communist government in FROM baltic country and they wish to be part puppet
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.5
	title = russia2_russia.5.t
	desc = russia2_russia.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_in_riga

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				save_event_target_as = baltic
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.5.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_subject = no }
			}
			SOV = { puppet = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = LIT } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = russia2_russia.5_threat_LIT }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FIN } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = russia2_russia.5_threat_FIN }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = EST } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = russia2_russia.5_threat_EST }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = LAT } }
				add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = russia2_russia.5_threat_LAT }
			}

		#trigger news event
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event =  { id = news.70 days = 1}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.5.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

#Finland want us to annex them
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.12
	title = russia2_russia.12.t
	desc = russia2_russia.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_tank_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept
		name = russia2_russia.12.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = FIN
				}
				SOV = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = FIN
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		add_threat = 1
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = news.69 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = russia2_russia.12.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}
}

# SOV recover territory
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.15
	title = russia2_russia.15.t
	desc = russia2_russia.15.d
	picture = GFX_soldiers_with_guns_russia2

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_idea = SOV_Exiled_russia
		195 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
		219 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
		217 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	option = { # Remove Exiled Russia
		name = russia2_russia.15.a
		remove_ideas = SOV_Exiled_russia
		add_stability = 0.20
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 2 id = newsrussia2.14 }
		}
	}
}

#White Death
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.19
	title = russia2_russia.19.t
	desc = russia2_russia.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_government = communism
		is_subject = no
		FIN = {
			AND = {
				surrender_progress > 0.05
				has_defensive_war_with = SOV
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = { #White death strike again !
		name = russia2_russia.19.a
		add_ideas = SOV_White_death
	}
}

#Train New Officers
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.20
	title = russia2_russia.20.t
	desc = russia2_russia.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_inspect_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#attack is the best defense
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = russia2_russia.20.a
		every_army_leader = {
			add_attack = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_attack
	}

	option = { #defense
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = russia2_russia.20.b
		every_army_leader = {
			add_defense = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_defense
	}

	option = { #logistic
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = russia2_russia.20.c
		every_army_leader = {
			add_logistics = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_logistics
	}

	option = { #planning
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		name = russia2_russia.20.e
		every_army_leader = {
			add_planning = 1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_New_officers_planning
	}
}

#KatyÅ„ Massacre
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.21
	title = russia2_russia.21.t
	desc = russia2_russia.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_army

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_government = communism
		is_subject = no
		has_country_leader = {
			character = SOV_Joseph_stalin
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		96 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		784 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		95 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		94 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		93 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		91 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
		89 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 8 }

	option = { #Do the massacre
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		name = russia2_russia.21.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Katyn_massacre
			days = 630
		}
		add_manpower = -22000
		set_country_flag = katyn_massacre
	}

	option = { #We're not monsters
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		name = russia2_russia.21.b
	}
}

#Germany Discovers the Massacre
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.22
	title = russia2_russia.22.t
	desc = russia2_russia.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_war_with = SOV
		controls_state = 242
		SOV = {
			has_country_flag = katyn_massacre
			has_government = communism
			is_subject = no
			has_country_leader = {
				character = SOV_Joseph_stalin
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = { #Mein Gott !
		name = russia2_russia.22.a
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = newsrussia2.23 }
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = denounced_katyn_massacre
			}
		}
		POL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = katyn_massacre
			}
		}
	}
}

# Great Purge - Begins
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.24
	title = russia2_russia.24.t
	desc = russia2_russia.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	timeout_days = 5

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.24.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_great_purge_begins_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = SOV_Great_purge
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_Genrikh_yagoda
				add_idea = SOV_Nikolay_yezhov
			}
		}
	}
}

# Great Purge - End
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.25
	title = russia2_russia.25.t
	desc = russia2_russia.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_purge_over
			communism_great_purge_variable_calculator = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.25.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						var = sov_great_purge_status^1
						value = 1
						compare = equals
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_great_purge_ends_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Nikolay_yezhov
					add_idea = SOV_Lavrentiy_beria
				}
				set_country_flag = SOV_Nikolay_yezhov_purged
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_great_purge_ends_tt2
			hidden_effect = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Nikolay_yezhov
					add_idea = SOV_Genrikh_yagoda
				}
				set_country_flag = SOV_Nikolay_yezhov_purged
			}
		}
	}
}

# Foreign Policies
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.28
	title = russia2_russia.28.t
	desc = russia2_russia.28.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Molotov
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = russia2_russia.28.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_great_purge_status^5
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = SOV_Vyacheslav_molotov
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = anti_capitalism_diplomacy }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = anti_capitalism_diplomacy_bonus }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_great_purge_status^5
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = only_molotov_available
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = newsrussia2.17 }
			set_country_flag = replaced_maisky
			set_country_flag = foreign_diplomacy_set
		}
	}

	option = { #Maisky
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = russia2_russia.28.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_great_purge_status^5
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = SOV_Ivan_maisky
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = anti_fascist_diplomacy }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = anti_fascist_diplomacy_bonus }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_great_purge_status^5
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = only_maisky_available
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = newsrussia2.18 }

country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.42
	title = russia2_russia.42.t
	desc = russia2_russia.42.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_officers_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Bribe his Guards
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = russia2_russia.42.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_bribe_guard
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_bribe_guard_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_low_kill_chance_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_low_risk_chance_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { random_factor_bribe = 0 }
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = random_factor_bribe
				distribution = uniform
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
			round_variable = random_factor_bribe
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_bribe
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.44 days = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_bribe
						value = 50
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.45 days = 20 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.46 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_bribe_guard
	}

	option = { #Send an Assassin

			factor = 10
		}

				var = random_factor_assassin
				distribution = uniform
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
			round_variable = random_factor_assassin
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_assassin
						value = 60
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.44 days = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_assassin
						value = 70
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.45 days = 20 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.46 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = SOV_send_assassin
	}

	option = { #Send the Squad

			factor = 80

#Assassination Sucessful
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.44
	title = russia2_russia.44.t
	desc = russia2_russia.44.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Perfect
		name = russia2_russia.44.a
		kill_country_leader = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Empty_supreme_soviet_soviet_union
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Empty_supreme_soviet_soviet_union_desc
				ideology = stalinism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					empty_parliament
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.34 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = SOV_bribe_guard
					NOT = { has_global_flag = SOV_try_again }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_military
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_send_assassin
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_military2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_send_squad
			}
		add_ideas = SOV_Payment_military3
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_armed_bureau
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_bureaucrats
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = SOV_bomb_bureau
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Payment_bureaucrats2
		}
		dismantle_faction = yes
	}
}

#The Assassination Attempt Failed
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.45
	title = russia2_russia.45.t
	desc = russia2_russia.45.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Damn
		name = russia2_russia.45.a
		set_global_flag = SOV_civil_war_peace
		set_country_flag = ENG_communist_civil_war
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = sov_fragmentation_status
					option = SOV_FRAGMENTED
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = communism
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.4
				capital = 260
				states = {
					260 240 220 224 222 258 257 239 255 250 205 223 254
				}
				keep_unit_leaders = {
					401 402 407 410 405 407
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = communism
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.4
				capital = 233
				states = {
					233 232 235 234 231 230 229 232 137 218 238 237 236 217 245
				}
				keep_unit_leaders = {
					401 402 407 410 406 405 403 407 404
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.88
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Empty_supreme_soviet_soviet_union
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Empty_supreme_soviet_soviet_union_desc
				ideology = stalinism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					empty_parliament
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_country_flag = ENG_communist_civil_war
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}	
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = STS
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = russia2_soviet_focus
					keep_completed = no
				}
				unlock_national_focus = SOV_great_purge2
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = SOV_communism_party
					name = SOV_communism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = SOV_communism_party
					name = SOV_communism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = SOV_communism_party
					name = SOV_communism_party
				}
				retire_ideology_leader = democratic
				retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
				retire_ideology_leader = fascism
			}
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.29 days = 1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_Instability2
				add_idea = SOV_Instability
			}
			set_global_flag = Trotsky_coming_back2
		}
	}
}

#Civil War
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.48
	title = russia2_russia.48.t
	desc = russia2_russia.48.d
	picture = GFX_artillery_with_building_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #For The Motherland !
		name = russia2_russia.48.a
		set_country_flag = ENG_communist_civil_war
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = sov_fragmentation_status
					option = SOV_FRAGMENTED
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = communism
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.5
				capital = 260
				states = {
					260 240 220 224 222 258 257 239 255 250 205 223 254
				}
				keep_unit_leaders = {
					401 402 407 410 405 407
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = communism
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.5
				capital = 217
				states = {
					217 260 265 240 401 407 402 404 732 742 405 584 585 587 406 236 237 238 234 218 228 217 245 236 237 238 234 235 232 233 231 229 230 586 589 227 221 200 226 137 196 259 203 198 192 197
				}
				keep_unit_leaders = {
					401 402 407 410 405 407
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.88
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Empty_supreme_soviet_soviet_union
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Empty_supreme_soviet_soviet_union_desc
				ideology = stalinism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					empty_parliament
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			dismantle_faction = yes
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_country_flag = ENG_communist_civil_war
				dismantle_faction = yes
				set_global_flag = SOV_end_civil_war
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = STS
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = russia2_soviet_focus
					keep_completed = no
				}
				unlock_national_focus = SOV_great_purge2
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = SOV_communism_party
					name = SOV_communism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = SOV_communism_party
					name = SOV_communism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = SOV_communism_party
					name = SOV_communism_party
				}
				retire_ideology_leader = democratic
				retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
				retire_ideology_leader = fascism
			}
			set_global_flag = Trotsky_coming_back2
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.30 days = 1 }
			remove_ideas = SOV_Army_disorganisation
		}
	}
}

#Stalin is Dead
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.59
	title = russia2_russia.59.t
	desc = russia2_russia.59.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.59.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Vasily_stalin
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Vasily_stalin_desc
				ideology = stalinism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					unplanned_sortie
					new_hope
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = { global.drunkard_wheel_achievement = THIS }
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { global.drunkard_wheel_achievement = THIS }
				set_variable = { global.drunkard_wheel_achievement_date@THIS = global.date }
				set_country_flag = russia_reworked_new_achievement
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = russia_reworked_achievements_enabled
					}
					scoped_sound_effect = "russia_reworked_unlock_achievement"
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.32 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.59.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_great_purge_status^6
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Nikita_khrushchev
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Nikita_khrushchev_desc
				ideology = stalinism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					secret_speech
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			UKR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						UKR_Nikita_khrushchev = {
							is_country_leader = yes
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						character = UKR_Vladimir_antonov_ovseyenko_communist
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							desc = UKR_Vladimir_antonov_ovseyenko_communist_desc
							ideology = marxism
							expire = "1965.1.1.1"
							traits = {
								
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.32 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.59.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_great_purge_status^1
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Lavrentiy_beria
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Lavrentiy_beria_desc
				ideology = stalinism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					
				}
			}

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.32 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

		remove_ideas = SOV_Suppressed_research
	}

#Ukrainian Anger
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.80
	title = russia2_russia.80.t
	desc = russia2_russia.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Would You Please Calm Down Thanks
		name = russia2_russia.80.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
			    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
			    value = 10
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
			    var = ukrainian_revolt_nothing_happens
			    value = 10
			}

			random_list = {
			    ukrainian_revolt_factor = {
			        country_event = { id = russia2_russia.81 days = 50 }
			    }
			    ukrainian_revolt_nothing_happens = {
			        country_event = { id = russia2_russia.80 days = 50 }
			    }
			    10 = {
			        country_event = { id = russia2_russia.82 days = 50 }
			    }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 25
				    compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_low_tt
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 25
				    compare = greater_than
				}
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 55
				    compare = less_than
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_medium_tt
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
				    var = ukrainian_revolt_factor
				    value = 55
				    compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_high_tt
		}

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 192 197 196 226 200 227 228 221 259 203 198 199 201 202 193 225 }
			limit = {
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = industrial_complex level > 0
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
			    type = industrial_complex damage = 1
			}
		}

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 192 197 196 226 200 227 228 221 259 203 198 199 201 202 193 225 }
			limit = {
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = arms_factory level > 0
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
			    type = arms_factory damage = 1
			}
		}

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 192 197 196 226 200 227 228 221 259 203 198 199 201 202 193 225 }
			limit = {
				non_damaged_building_level = {
					building = infrastructure level > 1
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
			    type = infrastructure
			    damage = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Ukrainian Revolt
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.81
	title = russia2_russia.81.t
	desc = russia2_russia.81.d
	picture = GFX_cavalry_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Uh Oh...
		name = russia2_russia.81.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_ukrainian_anger_revolt_tt

		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 202
						UKR = {
							exists = no
						}
					}
					UKR = {
						transfer_state = 202
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						UKR = {
							is_subject_of = SOV
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
					    target = UKR
					    autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_stability = -0.1
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = UKR
				}
				UKR = {
					army_experience = 25
					add_political_power = 150
					leave_faction = yes
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 10
						neutrality = 80
						fascism = 10
						communism = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
					}
					add_ideas = {
						SOV_Ukrainian_revolt
					}
					set_technology = {
						gw_artillery = 1
						tech_recon = 1
						tech_support = 1
						tech_engineers = 1
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Ukrainian Revolutionary Division"
						priority = 1
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
						}
						support = {
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							recon = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"2nd Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"3rd Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"4th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"5th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"6th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"7th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"8th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"9th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"10th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"11th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"12th Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" division_template = \"Ukrainian Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
							owner = UKR
						}
					}
				}

				SOV = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = UKR
						type = annex_everything
					}
					add_political_power = -50
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = UKR
							is_core_of = UKR
							NOT = {
								is_core_of = SOV
								state = 766
								state = 78
								state = 89
								state = 91
								state = 93 
							}
						}
						SOV = {
							add_state_core = PREV
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							UKR = {
								owns_state = 766
							}
						}
						add_state_claim = 766
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							UKR = {
								owns_state = 78
							}
						}
						add_state_claim = 78
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							UKR = {
								owns_state = 89
							}
						}
						add_state_claim = 89
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							UKR = {
								owns_state = 91
							}
						}
						add_state_claim = 91
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							UKR = {
								owns_state = 93
							}
						}
						add_state_claim = 93
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

#Form the Proletarian Union
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.86
	title = russia2_russia.86.t
	desc = russia2_russia.86.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes!
		name = russia2_russia.86.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = proletarian
		set_cosmetic_tag = SOV_proletarian_union
		set_country_flag = has_formed_proletarian_union
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_generic.4 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.42 days = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 42
				}
				set_capital = 42
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 16
				}
				set_capital = 16
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = { global.revolution_completed_achievement = THIS }
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { global.revolution_completed_achievement = THIS }
				set_variable = { global.revolution_completed_achievement_date@THIS = global.date }
				set_country_flag = russia_reworked_new_achievement
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = russia_reworked_achievements_enabled
					}
					scoped_sound_effect = "russia_reworked_unlock_achievement"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = { #Vasily Is the Leader

			factor = 100
		}

				name = "Vasily Stalin"

			}

			217 = {
				set_state_name = "Vasilygrad"
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Don't Change
		name = russia2_russia.94.i
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Leon Trotsky"

				}
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		SOV = {
			has_war = yes
			NOT = {
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
		}

			is_in_faction_with = SOV
			has_country_flag = unholy_alliance
			surrender_progress > 0.7
			has_war = yes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	option = { #Send the proposition
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		name = russia2_russia.97.a
		USA = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = russia2_america.4 }
		}
	}

	option = { #They can manage on their own

		name = russia2_russia.97.b
	}
}

	trigger = {
		original_tag = SOV

			is_ai = yes

				has_government = communism
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}

		}

		add_political_power = -150
	}

#Democratic Path - Reunification
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.108
	title = russia2_russia.108.t
	desc = russia2_russia.108.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 90
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.108.a
		FROM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.109 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = russian_investment@ROOT
				value = 3
				compare = not_equals
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				add = -30
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -60
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = {
					var = russian_investment@ROOT
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.108.b
		set_country_flag = sov_refused_reunification
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.110 }
		}
	}
}

#Second Civil War
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.131
	title = russia2_russia.131.t
	desc = russia2_russia.131.d
	picture = GFX_russian_civil_war_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = second_russian_civil_war_in_progress
			SOU = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SOV
					type = second_russian_civil_war
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					original_white_province_second_civil_war = no
					is_owned_by = SOU
				}
				SOV = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					original_white_province_second_civil_war = yes
				}
				SOU = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					UKR = {
						has_country_flag = accept_to_help_whiteguard
					}
				}
				UKR = {
					add_ideas = SOV_Second_civil_war_idea_modifier
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = SOV
						enemy = SOU
						hostility_reason = anti_soviet_alliance
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					SOU = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_ukraine.38 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_done
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.187 }
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.188 }
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.189 }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = newsrussia2.78 hours = 6
			}
		}
	}

	timeout_days = 5

	option = { #Civil War
		name = russia2_russia.131.a
	}
}

			value = 0
			compare = greater_than
		}
		#Add a country flag later, like has_country_flag = preparation_over
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

		name = russia2_russia.133.a

			amount = steal_weapons_final_count
			producer = SOV
		}

		multiply_temp_variable = { destroy_weapons_final_count = -1000 }
		SOU = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = destroy_weapons_final_count
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = steal_weaps
	}

#Sabotage Military Industry
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.134

	fire_only_once = yes

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = sabotage_mils
		has_global_flag = second_russian_civil_war_in_progress
		is_in_array = {
			array = sabotage_military_count
			value = 1
		}
		#Add a country flag later, like has_country_flag = preparation_over
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	immediate = {
		for_each_loop = {
			array = sabotage_military_count
			value = current #Should always be 1 for now, but can be useful in case we want to go deeper with the decisions
			index = i

			SOU = {
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						arms_factory > current
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = current
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = sabotage_mils
	}
}

#Russia Asks for Karelia
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.141
	title = russia2_russia.141.t
	desc = russia2_russia.141.d
	picture = GFX_cavalry_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.141.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			white_peace = {
				tag = SOV
				message = SURRENDER_KARELIA_MESSAGE
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.142 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 213
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_213_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 215
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_215_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 216
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_216_subject_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				all_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						state = 213
						state = 215
						state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.141.b
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.143 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 213
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_213_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 215
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_215_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 216
					NOT = {

					}

country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.142
	title = russia2_russia.142.t
	desc = russia2_russia.142.d
	picture = GFX_handshake_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Take back the Land
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = russia2_russia.142.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 213
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 213
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 215
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 215
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 216
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep them as a puppet
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = russia2_russia.142.b
		trigger = {
			KAR = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = FROM
				OR = {
					owns_state = 216
					owns_state = 215
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
		}
		puppet = KAR
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_freedom_all
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_russian_protectorate
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 215
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 216
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}
}

	title = russia2_russia.146.t
	desc = russia2_russia.146.d
	picture = GFX_military_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Doesn't give a wargoal because why would you declare war over Sakhalin?
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = russia2_russia.146.a
	}
}

#Reform the Entente
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.151
	title = russia2_russia.151.t
	desc = russia2_russia.151.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_pierre_laval

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.151.a
		SOV = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
					}
					SOV = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_faction = FRA
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.152 days = 1 }
		}
		FRA = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 500
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.151.b
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.254 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		name = russia2_russia.151.c
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.153 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Country Gets Event to Join to Entente
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.154
	title = russia2_russia.154.t
	desc = russia2_russia.154.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				add = -40
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					SOV = {
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.154.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
						is_faction_leader = yes
						NOT = {
							tag = SOV
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.257 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.155 days = 1 }
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					SOV = {
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.154.b
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.156 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Russia Asks for Karelia - Compromise
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.159
	title = russia2_russia.159.t
	desc = russia2_russia.159.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_second_vienna_award_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay - We want factories
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.159.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			white_peace = {
				tag = SOV
				message = SURRENDER_KARELIA_MESSAGE
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Received_karelia_payment
			days = 180
		}
		SOV = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = guarantee
				active = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.160 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 213
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_213_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 215
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_215_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 216
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_216_subject_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				all_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						state = 213
						state = 215
						state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		}
	}

	option = { #Okay - We want military aid
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.159.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			white_peace = {
				tag = SOV
				message = SURRENDER_KARELIA_MESSAGE
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Received_karelia_aid
			days = 180
		}
		SOV = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = guarantee
				active = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.161 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 213
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_213_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 215
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_215_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 216
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_216_subject_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				all_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						state = 213
						state = 215
						state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.159.c
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.162 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 213
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_213_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 215
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_215_subject_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 216
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_karelia_216_subject_tt
		}
	}
}

#We give back Karelia - Industry
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.160
	title = russia2_russia.160.t
	desc = russia2_russia.160.d
	picture = GFX_handshake_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = russia2_russia.160.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 213
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 213
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 215
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 215
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = {
						owns_state = 216
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = FROM
						owns_state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep them as a puppet
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = russia2_russia.160.b
		trigger = {
			KAR = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = FROM
				OR = {
					owns_state = 216
					owns_state = 215
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Karelia_payment
				days = 180
			}
		}
		puppet = KAR
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_freedom_all
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_russian_protectorate
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KAR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 213
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 213
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 215
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 215
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 216
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}
}

#We give back Karelia - Military
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.161
	title = russia2_russia.161.t
	desc = russia2_russia.161.d

				}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					owns_state = 216
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 216
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = FROM
					OR = {
						owns_state = 213
						owns_state = 215
						owns_state = 216
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = PREV
					generator = { 213 215 216 }
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = FROM
			generator = { 213 215 216 }
		}
	}
}

#Russia Asks for North Sakhalin
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.163
	title = russia2_russia.163.t
	desc = russia2_russia.163.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		name = russia2_russia.163.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Received_sakhalin_payment
			days = 180
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			white_peace = {
				tag = SOV
				message = SURRENDER_NORTH_SAKHALIN_MESSAGE
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			transfer_state = 655
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.164 days = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					owns_state = 655
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
 			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_sakhalin_subject_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				all_owned_state = {
					state = 655
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		name = russia2_russia.163.b
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.165 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Russian Culture Promoted!
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.166
	title = russia2_russia.166.t
	desc = russia2_russia.166.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_crowd_in_prague

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = russian_culture_promote
		set_country_flag = receive_promote_russian_culture_event
	}

	option = { #Okay
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SOV = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_freedom_all
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.166.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.167 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No, only if a player somehow wants to play a Russian State OR the Reunification was not completed
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				SOV = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_freedom_all
				}
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.166.b
	}
}

#FROM Gets Annexed
country_event = {

					tag = LAT

						tag = SOV
						tag = MAC
					}
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50

					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}

		}

				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 500
			}

				value = 2
			}
		}

					}
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}

#End of the Civil War - Aftermath
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.190
	title = russia2_russia.190.t
	desc = russia2_russia.190.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.190.a
		set_global_flag = second_russian_civil_war_over
		clr_global_flag = second_russian_civil_war_in_progress
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			add_ideas = SOV_Isolation
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_civil_war_focus
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						country_exists = UKR
						UKR = {
							has_completed_focus = UKR_boost_industry
						}
					}
				}
				UKR = {
					add_offsite_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = -1
					}
					add_offsite_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = -2
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
							has_country_flag = has_negotiated_with_germany_ressource_rights
							has_country_flag = accept_american_occupation_siberia_after_cw 
							has_country_flag = accept_french_factories_after_cw 
							has_country_flag = accept_diplomatic_relation_with_italy 
							has_country_flag = accept_english_help_for_shipment 
						}
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_generic.34 days = 7 }
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOU
				}
				remove_core_of = SOU
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_central_asia
				}
				KAZ = {
					transfer_state = 406
					transfer_state = 407
					transfer_state = 589
					transfer_state = 588
				}
			}
			582 = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = urals_secret
				}
			}
			573 = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = urals_secret
				}
			}
			581 = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = urals_secret
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Opytnyy Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 50000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -50000
				}	
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 40000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 50000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -40000
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 30000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 40000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -30000
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 20000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 30000
					}
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -20000
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						TAG = SOV
						TAG = UKR
						TAG = BLR
						TAG = AZR
						TAG = GER
						TAG = ARM
						TAG = KAZ
						TAG = TMS
						TAG = CRI
					}
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Yaponskiy Dobrovol'cheskiy Diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Ital'yanskiy Dobrovol'cheskiy Diviziya"
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						TAG = UKR
						TAG = BLR
						TAG = AZR
						TAG = GER
						TAG = ARM
						TAG = KAZ
						TAG = TMS
						TAG = CRI
					}
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Opytnyy Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "gvardeyskaya pekhotnaya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Gvardeyskaya kavaleriyskaya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Panzer Diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Diviziya Morskoy Pekhoty"
				}
			}
		}
		add_threat = -5
		remove_ideas = SOV_Supply_line
		remove_ideas = SOV_Second_civil_war_idea_modifier
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Second_civil_war_idea_modifier
				}
				remove_ideas = SOV_Second_civil_war_idea_modifier
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = SOV_Urals_secret
		remove_ideas = SOV_Slow_industry
		dismantle_faction = yes
		add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
		add_ideas = SOV_Political_Unstability
	}
}

#SOU Annex SOV puppets if it's AI controlled and almost at 100% surrender
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.191

	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = SOU
		has_war = yes
		SOV = {
			exists = yes
			surrender_progress > 0.75
			has_country_flag = sov_near_capitulation
			is_ai = yes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOU = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Contact the German Exiles
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.192
	title = russia2_russia.192.t
	desc = russia2_russia.192.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fascist_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = russia2_russia.192.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		set_temp_variable = { random_factor_german_exilee = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_factor_german_exilee
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_factor_german_exilee
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_german_exilee
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.193 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.194 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Germany shall never be unified again
		name = russia2_russia.192.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = choosing_this_option_destroy_german_unification
		set_country_flag = decide_to_restore_prussia_and_other_kingdom
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.192.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

		round_variable = random_factor_german_exilee2
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_german_exilee2
						value = 75
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.195 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.196 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Ask one more time
		name = russia2_russia.194.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		set_temp_variable = { random_factor_german_exilee = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_factor_german_exilee
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_factor_german_exilee
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = random_factor_german_exilee
						value = 50
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.193 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.196 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Ok then, bye
		name = russia2_russia.194.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#Hidden Event to trigger when the player select compensate generals
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.207

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { random_generals_2 = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_generals_2
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_generals_2
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_2
					value = 20
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Georgy Zhukov"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Georgy_Zhukov.dds"
					traits = { winter_specialist armor_officer media_personality war_hero }
					skill = 5
					attack_skill = 5
					defense_skill = 2
					planning_skill = 4
					logistics_skill = 5
				}
				clr_country_flag = sov_enemy_second_civil_war_georgy_zhu
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_2
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Yakov Cherevichenko"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Yakov_Cherevichenko.dds"
					traits = { cavalry_officer }
					skill = 3
					attack_skill = 3
					defense_skill = 3
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Markian Popov"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Matkian_Popov.dds"
					traits = { winter_specialist infantry_officer brilliant_strategist }
					skill = 2
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Hidden Event to trigger when the player select compensate generals - 2
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.208

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { random_generals_3 = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_generals_3
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_generals_3
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_3
					value = 20
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Ivan Konev"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Ivan_Konev.dds"
					traits = { armor_officer harsh_leader politically_connected }
					skill = 5
					attack_skill = 4
					defense_skill = 5
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 5
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = sov_enemy_second_civil_war_konev
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_3
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Kirill Meretskov"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Kirill_Meretskov.dds"
					traits = { trait_reckless infantry_officer }
					skill = 3
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 2
					planning_skill = 3
					logistics_skill = 3
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Ivan Fedyuninsky"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Ivan_Fedyuninsky.dds"
					traits = { infantry_officer }
					skill = 1
					attack_skill = 1
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.209

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { random_generals_4 = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = random_generals_4
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = random_generals_4
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_4
					value = 20
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Aleksandr Vasilevsky"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Aleksandr_Vasilevsky.dds"
					traits = { armor_officer politically_connected }
					skill = 4
					attack_skill = 4
					defense_skill = 4
					planning_skill = 3
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = sov_enemy_second_civil_war_vasilevsky
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_generals_4
					value = 60
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Maksim Purkayev"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Maksim_Purkayev.dds"
					traits = { career_officer }
					skill = 3
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 3
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 3
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				create_field_marshal = {
					name = "Grigory Kulik"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Grigory_Kulik.dds"
					traits = { old_guard career_officer politically_connected inflexible_strategist }
					skill = 1
					attack_skill = 1
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = russia2_russia.210.a

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = TSAR_NEUTRALITY
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = JUNTA_NEUTRALITY
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = monarchist_restoration_possible
		set_country_flag = monarchist_restoration_path
	}

	option = { #Become Junta
		name = russia2_russia.210.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = TSAR_NEUTRALITY
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = JUNTA_NEUTRALITY
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = military_junta_possible
		set_country_flag = military_junta_leader
	}
}

#Vassalization of Ukraine - Reintegrate the Lost State
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.213
	title = russia2_russia.213.t
	desc = russia2_russia.213.d
	picture = GFX_cavalry_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accepts and Become Puppets
		name = russia2_russia.213.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = imperial_annexation_lost
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = UKR
					autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.214 hours = 6 }
			}
			UKR = {
				set_country_flag = ukraine_no_imperial_govern
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = SOV_Tsar_we_trust
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = UKR
						autonomy_state = autonomy_imperial_governorates
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = UKR
						autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.214 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = SOV_Isolation
	}

	option = { #Refuse and Stay Independent - Gets National Spirit
		name = russia2_russia.213.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SOV = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.215 hours = 6 }
		}
		set_country_flag = ukr_refused_vassalization_process
		UKR = {
			add_ideas = SOV_Fight_for_independence
		}
	}
}

#Tsar's Death. His Son Takes Over
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.226
	title = russia2_russia.226.t
	desc = russia2_russia.226.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			character = SOV_Kirill_vladimirovich
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = sov_old_tsar_still_alive
			days > 365
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days =  10
	}

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.226.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			retire_character = SOV_Kirill_vladimirovich
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_tsar_kirill_dies
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Vladimir_kirillovich
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Vladimir_kirillovich_desc
				ideology = despotism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					russia2_heir_of_the_tsar
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Option to Cedes South Sakhalin to Japan if In Second Civil War
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.227
	title = russia2_russia.227.t
	desc = {
		text = russia2_russia.227.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
			}	
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = russia2_russia.227.d_2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
			}
		}
	} 
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ask Non-Aggression Pact for North Sakhalin
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.227.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_japan.8 hours = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Never
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
			}	
		}
		name = russia2_russia.227.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	option = { #Give Them due to the Deal
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_north_sakhalin
				has_country_flag = japan_accept_to_help_give_russian_far_east
			}
		}
		name = russia2_russia.227.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		JAP = {
			transfer_state = 655
			JAP = {
				add_ideas = SOV_Japan_non_agression_pact_sakhalin
			}
		}
	}
}

#Russian Ultimatum to Return the Land of Germany
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.229
	title = russia2_russia.229.t
	desc = russia2_russia.229.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Return the Land
		name = russia2_russia.229.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				add = -40
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GER
			}
			GER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.230 hours = 6 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Never
		name = russia2_russia.229.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GER
			}
			PREV.PREV = {
				add_resistance = 50
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.231 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}

#Cannot Reinstore the German Monarchy - Player Gets Event Telling Him What to do
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.232
	title = russia2_russia.232.t
	desc = russia2_russia.232.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Send Ultimatum
		name = russia2_russia.232.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
				GER = {
					is_subject_of = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.233 days = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Declare War
		name = russia2_russia.232.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		SOV = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = GER
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Do Nothing
		name = russia2_russia.232.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = anger_german_monarchist
		clr_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
		clr_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
		clr_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
	}

#Russian Ultimatum to Cede Germany

	desc = russia2_russia.233.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Cede Germany
		name = russia2_russia.233.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					is_subject_of = PREV
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = GER
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.234 hours = 6 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Never
		name = russia2_russia.233.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = war_over_germany_overlord
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.235 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}

#Event for SOU to Release SOV if it Wins the Civil War
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.238
	title = russia2_russia.238.t
	desc = russia2_russia.238.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_finnish_soldiers_snow

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.238.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = UKR
				is_owned_by = UKR
			}
			SOV = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = UKR
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = UKR
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = POL
						is_owned_by = ROM
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}	 
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SOV
				any_country = {
					owns_state = PREV
					NOT = {
						TAG = SOV
						TAG = TAN
						TAG = JAP
						TAG = UKR
						TAG = CRI
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			set_country_flag = white_guard_lost_civil_war
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
			}

			add_ideas = SOV_Suppressed_research

						TAG = JAP

				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

#France Asks for Leadership
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.254
	title = russia2_russia.254.t
	desc = russia2_russia.254.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_worried_french

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		name = russia2_russia.254.a
		FRA = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				set_faction_name = entente_reformed
			}
			else = {
				create_faction = entente_reformed
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
					FRA = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_faction = SOV
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.255 days = 1 }
		}
		FRA = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = SOV
				value = 500
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		name = russia2_russia.254.b
		FRA = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.256 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
			has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
		}		
		GER = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}		
		}
		85 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
		}
		86 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
		}
	}

	option = { #Return German Lands
		name = russia2_russia.259.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		GER = {
			transfer_state = 86
			transfer_state = 85
			add_state_core = 85
			add_state_core = 86
		}
	}

	option = { #Don't Return German Lands
		name = russia2_russia.259.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = {
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = anger_germany_poland_deal
			hidden_effect = {
				GER = {
					add_ideas = SOV_German_independence_movement
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			GER = {
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

							has_country_flag = accept_english_help_for_shipment

			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOU
				}
				remove_core_of = SOU
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_central_asia
				}
				KAZ = {
					transfer_state = 406
					transfer_state = 407
					transfer_state = 589
					transfer_state = 588
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_central_asia
				}
				KAZ = {
					transfer_state = 590
					transfer_state = 583
					transfer_state = 402
					transfer_state = 587
				}
				remove_state_core = 590
				remove_state_core = 583
				remove_state_core = 402
				remove_state_core = 587
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Opytnyy Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = train_caucasian_soldiers_civil_war
					has_country_flag = control_caucasus
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Opytnyy Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Kavkazskaya kazach'ya diviziya"
				}

				remove_dynamic_modifier = {

				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = urals_secret
				}

					}
				}

					type = infantry_equipment

				}

					division_template = "Ital'yanskiy Dobrovol'cheskiy Diviziya"

					}

				}

				set_country_flag = mikhail_deserted
			}

		}	
	}
