#Return of Konstantin
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.280
	title = russia2_russia.280.t
	desc = russia2_russia.280.d
	picture = GFX_konstantin_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.280.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_Uncertain_fate
		add_ideas = SOV_Russian_hypernationalism
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = RFP
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.282 days = 100 }
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.114 days = 1 } 
		}
	}
}

#The Fate of Anastasy
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.282
	title = russia2_russia.282.t
	desc = russia2_russia.282.d
	picture = GFX_russia2event_anastasy_vonsiatsky

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept his return
		name = russia2_russia.282.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.283 days = 100 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep small contacts with him
		name = russia2_russia.282.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.290 days = 100 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse his return
		name = russia2_russia.282.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
				NOT = {
					controls_state = 366
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.298 days = 100 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Demand the controller of 366 (Florida) to arrest him

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 366
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			366 = {
				CONTROLLER = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.305 days = 50 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Arrest him
		name = russia2_russia.282.f
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 366
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = ANASTASY_FASCIST
				}

				add = 90
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
				controls_state = 366
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.309 days = 50 }
		}
		#This is just in case you control 366, very unlikely
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_fascist_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.286.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		set_temp_variable = { konstantin_death_factor = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = konstantin_death_factor
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 2
		}
		round_variable = konstantin_death_factor
		if = { #Dead
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = konstantin_death_factor
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.287 days = 50 }
			}
		}
		else = { #Not dead
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.288 days = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = russia2_russia.291.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		add_stability = -0.05

		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = konstantin_death_factor
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 4
		}
		round_variable = konstantin_death_factor
		if = { #Dead
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = konstantin_death_factor

				}
			}

			}
		}

			var = konstantin_death_factor

			max = 4
		}
		round_variable = konstantin_death_factor

		name = russia2_russia.298.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		set_temp_variable = { konstantin_death_factor = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = konstantin_death_factor
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 4
		}
		round_variable = konstantin_death_factor
		if = { #Dead
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = konstantin_death_factor
					value = 3
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.300 days = 75 }
			}
		}
		else = { #Not dead
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.299 days = 50 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Who cares
		name = russia2_russia.298.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_ai_behavior
					option = KONSTANTIN_FASCIST
				}
			}
		}

#Broken ROOT-Russian Agreement
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.313
	title = russia2_russia.313.t
	desc = russia2_russia.313.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_lend_lease

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = SOV_Root_russian_pact
		}
	}

	option = { #Oh
		name = russia2_russia.313.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_offensive_war_with = SOV
			}
			set_temp_variable = { stability_loss_fascism_factor = ROOT.party_popularity@fascism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { stability_loss_fascism_factor = -1 }
			clamp_temp_variable = {
				var = stability_loss_fascism_factor
				min = -0.25
				max = -0.1
			}
			add_stability = stability_loss_fascism_factor
		}
		else = { #Won't punish the player too hard if SOV is the attacker
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				country_event = russia2_russia.314
			}
			clr_country_flag = accepted_russian_root_agreement
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = is_target_of_russia_with_agreement
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = support
						id = PREV
						value = 1000
					}

					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = 1000
					}

					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = send_volunteers_desire
						id = PREV
						value = 1000
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Undo the hostile behaviors towards Russian enemies
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.317
	
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = accepted_russian_root_agreement
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = is_target_of_russia_with_agreement
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = PREV
					value = 1000
				}

				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = PREV
					value = 1000
				}

				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = send_volunteers_desire
					id = PREV
					value = 1000
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Used for AI strategy, should work fine now, using event instead of on_action to avoid bugs and performance issues
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.318
	
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			SOV = {
				AND = {
					has_war = yes
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes
						days > 7
					}
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = {
				flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes_global
				days > 15
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes
		set_country_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes
		clr_global_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes_global
		set_global_flag = SOV_ai_strategy_count_enemy_planes_global
		set_variable = { plane_count_enemy_sov = 0 }
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = SOV.enemies
			break = end_array
			
			set_temp_variable = { temp_var_plane_count = num_deployed_planes }
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { plane_count_enemy_sov = temp_var_plane_count }
			}
		}
	}
}

#The fate of FROM
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.319
	title = russia2_russia.319.t
	desc = russia2_russia.319.d
	picture = GFX_military_parade_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Demande puppet
		name = russia2_russia.319.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		event_target:SOV_target_country_fascist = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.320 days = 1 }
		}
		#clear_global_event_target = SOV_target_country_fascist
		#Resets anyways, and causes errors for the next events for some reasons
	}

	option = { #Demande annex
		name = russia2_russia.319.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		event_target:SOV_target_country_fascist = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.323 days = 1 }
		}
		#clear_global_event_target = SOV_target_country_fascist
	}

	option = { #Enforce military access
		name = russia2_russia.319.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		event_target:SOV_target_country_fascist = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.326 days = 1 }
		}
		#clear_global_event_target = SOV_target_country_fascist
	}
}

#SOV Demands Puppet
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.320
	title = russia2_russia.320.t
	desc = russia2_russia.320.d
	picture = GFX_artillery_with_building_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ok
		name = russia2_russia.320.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -40
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				is_major = no
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_idea = SOV_Impose_order
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_state_magistrate
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.321 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.321 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.141 days = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.320.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				is_major = no
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.322 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.144 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = russia2_russia.323.d

		name = russia2_russia.323.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				is_major = no
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_game_totally_over_TT
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.140 }
		}
		SOV = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = no
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.324 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.323.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				is_major = yes

				add = 50

						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
					any_country = {
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.143 }

		}
	}
}

			factor = 100
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = can_cancel_military_access_from_SOV
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				country_event = russia2_russia.332
			}
		}
	}
}

#Tsar Marriage
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.333
	title = russia2_russia.333.t
	desc = russia2_russia.333.d
	picture = GFX_royal_marriage_tsar_russia2

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		date > 1938.01.01
	}

	option = { #Yay
		name = russia2_russia.333.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = tsar_marriage_happened
	}
}

#Lost State Receive Events to be Integreated Back to Russia
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.335
	title = russia2_russia.335.t
	desc = russia2_russia.335.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_south_africa_patrol

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yay
		name = russia2_russia.335.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		SOV = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.336 hours = 12 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.335.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.337 hours = 12 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_ideas = SOV_Fighting_against_the_russians
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_lost_state = yes
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_lost_state = yes
					exists = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

#Event for Germany (Memories)
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.338
	title = russia2_russia.338.t
	desc = russia2_russia.338.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fascist_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ask for a treaty of friendship
		name = russia2_russia.338.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		trigger = {
			GER = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.339 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Announce hostility
		name = russia2_russia.338.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = hostile_russian_german_relations
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.342 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Russo-German Treaty
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.339
	title = russia2_russia.339.t
	desc = russia2_russia.339.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = russia2_russia.339.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Russo_german_treaty_fascist
			days = 180
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = SOV
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = accepted_russo_german_treaty
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.340 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.339.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = refused_russo_german_treaty
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.341 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			ruling_party = fascism
		}

			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.2

			set_cosmetic_tag = RFP

		}
	}
}

#Konstantin was executed and Anastasy takes over
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.344
	title = russia2_russia.344.t
	desc = russia2_russia.344.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #If Konstantin is executed, Anastasy is supposed to take over anyways
		name = russia2_russia.344.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_can_have_anastasy_tt
		set_country_flag = order_triumphed_over_law
		add_ideas = SOV_Uncertain_fate
		add_ideas = SOV_Russian_hypernationalism
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.2
		}

#Profit from FROM (Russian States)
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.360
	title = russia2_russia.360.t
	desc = russia2_russia.360.d
	picture = GFX_military_parade_kremlin_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Great!
		name = russia2_russia.360.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_variable = { economicgainfactor = 0 }
		randomize_variable = {
			var = economicgainfactor
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0.5
			max = 3.5
		}
		round_variable = economicgainfactor
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = economicgainfactor
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = economicgainfactor
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = economicgainfactor
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Send Profit to SOV
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.361

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			set_temp_variable = { nexteconomicevent = 0 }
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = nexteconomicevent
				distribution = uniform
				min = 100
				max = 365
			}
			round_temp_variable = nexteconomicevent
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.360 days = var:nexteconomicevent }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Communist Ultimatum
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.367
	title = russia2_russia.367.t
	desc = russia2_russia.367.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_in_riga

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = communist_ultimatum_triggered
			remove_ideas = SOV_Communist_influence_international_3
			clr_country_flag = SOV_AI_is_target_international
			SOV = {
				clr_country_flag = SOV_AI_is_influencing_international
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Civil war
		name = russia2_russia.367.a
		trigger = {
			num_of_controlled_states > 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = ROOT
			ideology = communism
			size = party_popularity@communism
		}
		set_country_flag = is_civil_war_international
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.145 hours = 5 }
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.370 }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = communism
					original_tag = ROOT
					any_country = {
						has_war_with = PREV
						has_civil_war = yes
						has_country_flag = communist_ultimatum_triggered
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = is_communist_triggered_revolution
				add_ideas = SOV_Supporters_fourth_international
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Submit
		name = russia2_russia.367.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communism
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_Supporters_fourth_international
		set_country_flag = submit_communism_international
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.149 hours = 5 }
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.371 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = { #Let's go
		name = russia2_russia.370.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_decision_can_puppet_communist_uprising
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { sov_trotsky_successful_revolution_count = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = sov_trotsky_successful_revolution_count
							value = 5
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						NOT = {
							is_in_array = { global.quick_revolution_achievement = THIS }
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { global.quick_revolution_achievement = THIS }
					set_variable = { global.quick_revolution_achievement_date@THIS = global.date }
					set_country_flag = russia_reworked_new_achievement
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_flag = russia_reworked_achievements_enabled
						}
						scoped_sound_effect = "russia_reworked_unlock_achievement"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = russia2_russia.383.t
	desc = russia2_russia.383.d
	picture = GFX_soldiers_with_guns_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #UHH
		name = russia2_russia.383.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = yes
				}
				OVERLORD = {
					country_event = russia2_russia.388
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ROOT
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Cold_civil_war
			days = 180
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = ROOT
			ideology = communism
			size = party_popularity@communism
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = newsrussia2.147 hours = 5 }
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.384 }
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = communism
					original_tag = ROOT
					any_country = {
						has_war_with = PREV
						has_civil_war = yes
						has_country_flag = civil_war_iron_curtain
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = is_communist_civil_war_iron_curtain
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SOV_Cold_civil_war
					days = 180
				}
				SOV = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = send_volunteers_desire
						id = PREV
						value = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Terrorist Anarchist are Wreaking Havoc
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.402
	title = russia2_russia.402.t
	desc = russia2_russia.402.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Those Damn Terrorists !
		name = russia2_russia.402.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_Anarchist_terrorist
		remove_ideas = trotskyite_plot_russia2_idea
		remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants1
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants2
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants3
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants4
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants5
			remove_ideas = SOV_Unhappy_peasants6
		}	
	}
}

#Hidden Event to spawn the Divisions and ships for the Black Revolution
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.404

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		SOV = {
			load_oob = "SOV_black_revolution_oob"
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_leningrad_ships"
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}	
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_leningrad_ships_nomtg"
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution_nomtg"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}	
				}
				load_oob = "SOV_naval_ships_black_revolution_nomtg"
			}
		}
		SOU = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = anarchist_soldiers_desert
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_black_revolution"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						has_country_flag = anarchist_soldiers_desert
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_black_revolution_deserted_version"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_naval_ships_black_revolution"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
					SOV = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = anarchist_hold_leningrad
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "SOU_naval_ships_black_revolution_nomtg"
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_trials_begin
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.422 days = 30 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Very well
		name = russia2_russia.409.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

#First Trial - Fate of the Syndicates
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.410
	title = russia2_russia.410.t
	desc = russia2_russia.410.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_fate_syndicates
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.426 days = 15 }
		}
	}

	option = { #They are clearly Communist
		name = russia2_russia.410.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}

	option = { #We will take control over them
		name = russia2_russia.410.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_to_variable = { united_russia_strength = 1 }
		round_variable = united_russia_strength
		clamp_variable = {
			var = united_russia_strength
			min = 0
			max = 4
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = united_russia_gains_strength
	}

	option = { #We will let them operate, the workers need the Syndicates
		name = russia2_russia.410.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { united_russia_strength = 1 }
		round_variable = united_russia_strength
		clamp_variable = {
			var = united_russia_strength
			min = 0
			max = 4
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = united_russia_lose_strength
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.10
		}
	}
}

#End of the Black Revolution - Civil War
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.412
	title = russia2_russia.412.t
	desc = russia2_russia.412.d
	picture = GFX_soldiers_with_guns_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.412.a
		set_country_flag = end_of_the_revolution
		clr_country_flag = black_revolution_civil_war_in_progress
		add_ideas = SOV_no_export_anarchy
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_revolution_focus_available
		custom_effect_tooltip = division_will_be_locked_anarchy
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOU
				}
				remove_core_of = SOU
			}
		}
		add_threat = -5
		remove_ideas = SOV_Determination
		black_revolution_division_template_organiser = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_Surprise_attack_black_revolution
			}
			remove_ideas = SOV_Surprise_attack_black_revolution
		}
	}
}

#Aftermath of the Coup - Black Revolution
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.413
	title = russia2_russia.413.t
	desc = russia2_russia.413.d
	picture = GFX_artillery_with_building_russia2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.413.a
		set_country_flag = end_of_the_revolution
		clr_country_flag = black_revolution_civil_war_in_progress
		add_ideas = SOV_no_export_anarchy
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_revolution_focus_available
		custom_effect_tooltip = division_will_be_locked_anarchy
		hidden_effect = {
			set_division_template_lock = {
				division_template = "Strelkovaya Diviziya"
				is_locked = yes
			}
			create_field_marshal = {
				name = "Supreme Military Council"
				picture = "Portrait_military_council.dds"
				traits = { winter_specialist logistics_wizard aggressive_assaulter }
				skill = 3
				attack_skill = 3
				defense_skill = 3
				planning_skill = 2
				logistics_skill = 2
			}
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Military Council of Ukraine"
				picture = "Portrait_military_council.dds"
				traits = { infantry_officer armor_officer }
				skill = 4
				attack_skill = 4
				defense_skill = 4
				planning_skill = 5
				logistics_skill = 4
			}
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Military Council of Belarus"

				traits = { ranger brilliant_strategist }
				skill = 3

#Hidden Event to create state flag for Send Recon Units without making a mess
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.414

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { sov_count_state_recon = 0 }
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = sov_count_state_recon
					value = 80
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			
			random_scope_in_array = {
				array = SOV.owned_controlled_states
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = recon_units_scout_place
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_1
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_2
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_3
						has_state_flag = medium_counter_revolution_resistance_1
						has_state_flag = medium_counter_revolution_resistance_2
						has_state_flag = large_counter_revolution_resistance_1
						state = 219
						state = 137
						state = 195
						state = 217
						state = 408
						state = 202
					}
				}
				
				remove_from_array = { SOV.sov_recon_rebel_anarchy_states = THIS }
				THIS = {
					set_state_flag = recon_units_scout_place
				}
			}

			add_to_variable = { sov_count_state_recon = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Result of Forced Quota - Industry 
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.420
	title = russia2_russia.420.t
	desc = russia2_russia.420.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #they worked well
		name = russia2_russia.420.a
		
	}

	option = { #More Work
		name = russia2_russia.420.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = this_could_bite_us_back
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					set_country_flag = worker_catastrophe_1
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.440  days = 15 }
				}
				60 = {
					set_country_flag = has_forced_work_not_failed_1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						}

						limit = {
							has_global_flag = russia_reworked_achievements_enabled

		}
	}

	}

	option = { #Put him in prison

#Country gets slavic help from SOV
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.505
	title = russia2_russia.505.t
	desc = russia2_russia.505.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_physics_lab_02

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { random_resource_slavic = 0 }
			randomize_variable = {
				var = random_resource_slavic
				distribution = uniform
				min = 1
				max = 6
			}
			round_variable = random_resource_slavic
		}
	}

	option = { #Cool
		name = russia2_russia.505.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = russian_help_slavic
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction  = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction  = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_resource_slavic
					value = 1
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = oil
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_resource_slavic
					value = 2
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = aluminium
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_resource_slavic
					value = 3
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = rubber
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_resource_slavic
					value = 4
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = tungsten
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_resource_slavic
					value = 5
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = random_resource_slavic
					value = 6
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = chromium
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Give Territory to KUR
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.506
	title = russia2_russia.506.t
	desc = russia2_russia.506.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accept
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.506.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					is_subject = yes
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = SOV
						ratio < 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUR
					is_claimed_by = KUR
				}
			}
			KUR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = russia2_russia.507
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			KUR = {
				country_event = russia2_russia.507
			}
		}
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.506.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_subject = yes
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = SOV
						ratio < 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				NOT = {
					tag = SOV
					tag = KUR
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_subject = yes
						}
						OVERLORD = {
							OR = {
								tag = SOV
								is_in_faction_with = SOV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = russia2_russia.508
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			KUR = {
				country_event = russia2_russia.508
			}
		}
	}
}

# Grand Duchess Anastasia Nikolaevna of Russia Returns (Anna Anderson)
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.509
	title = russia2_russia.509.t
	desc = russia2_russia.509.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	timeout_days = 2

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_government = neutrality
					is_subject = no
					has_capitulated = no
					has_completed_focus = SOV_restoration_tsar
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Kirill Vladimirovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SOV_the_emperor
						has_completed_focus = SOV_the_empress
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Anastasia Nikolaevna"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.510 days = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Oh hi
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.509.a
		set_country_flag = sov_anna_anderson_returns_russia
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_decisions_anna_anderson
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_met_princess_irene
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_government = neutrality
					is_subject = no
					has_capitulated = no
					has_completed_focus = SOV_restoration_tsar
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Kirill Vladimirovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SOV_the_emperor
						has_completed_focus = SOV_the_empress
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Anastasia Nikolaevna"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.511 days = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Recognized
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.510.a
		add_to_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		set_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = anna_anderson_legitimacy }
		multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 2 }
		round_variable = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui
		clamp_variable = {
			var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
			min = 0
			max = 200
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = anna_anderson_add_legitimacy_5
		set_country_flag = sov_met_princess_irene_yes
		add_stability = 0.05
	}

	#Not Recognized
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.510.b
		subtract_from_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		set_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = anna_anderson_legitimacy }
		multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 2 }
		round_variable = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui
		clamp_variable = {
			var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
			min = 0
			max = 200
		}	
		custom_effect_tooltip = anna_anderson_remove_legitimacy_5
		set_country_flag = sov_met_princess_irene_no
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

# Meeting with Prince Felix Felixovich Yusupov
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.511
	title = russia2_russia.511.t
	desc = russia2_russia.511.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_met_prince_felix
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_government = neutrality
					is_subject = no
					has_capitulated = no
					has_completed_focus = SOV_restoration_tsar
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Kirill Vladimirovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SOV_the_emperor
						has_completed_focus = SOV_the_empress
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Anastasia Nikolaevna"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.512 days = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Recognized
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.511.a
		add_to_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		set_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = anna_anderson_legitimacy }
		multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 2 }
		round_variable = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui
		clamp_variable = {
			var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
			min = 0
			max = 200
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = anna_anderson_add_legitimacy_5
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_country_flag = sov_met_prince_felix_yes
	}

	#Not Recognized
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.511.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
					value = 0.5
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy = 0.07 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			set_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = anna_anderson_legitimacy }
			multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 100 }
			multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 2 }
			round_variable = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui
			clamp_variable = {
				var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
				min = 0
				max = 200
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = anna_anderson_remove_legitimacy_7
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy = 0.03 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			set_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = anna_anderson_legitimacy }
			multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 100 }
			multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 2 }
			round_variable = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui
			clamp_variable = {
				var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
				min = 0
				max = 200
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = anna_anderson_remove_legitimacy_3
		}
		set_country_flag = sov_met_prince_felix_no
	}

	#He left unsure
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.511.c
		add_political_power = -200
		set_country_flag = sov_met_prince_felix_unsure
	}
}

# Anna Anderson Wins
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.515
	title = russia2_russia.515.t
	desc = russia2_russia.515.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = sov_anna_anderson_struggle_over
		set_country_flag = sov_anna_anderson_win
	}
	
	#Anastasia!
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.515.a
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = SOV_Anastasia_nikolaevna
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = SOV_Anastasia_nikolaevna_desc
				ideology = despotism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {
					saint_grand_duchess_and_passion_bearer
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = { global.not_sus_achievement = THIS }
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { global.not_sus_achievement = THIS }
				set_variable = { global.not_sus_achievement_date@THIS = global.date }
				set_country_flag = russia_reworked_new_achievement
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = russia_reworked_achievements_enabled
					}
					scoped_sound_effect = "russia_reworked_unlock_achievement"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# SOV wants to purchase african colony
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.516
	title = russia2_russia.516.t
	desc = russia2_russia.516.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				save_event_target_as = sov_african_state_purchase
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Ok
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.516.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				FROM.FROM = {
					state = 268
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = SOV_Selling_africa
					}
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SOV_Selling_africa
					days = 30
				}
			}
			else = {
				modify_timed_idea = {
					idea = SOV_Selling_africa
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
		FROM.FROM = {
			SOV = {
				country_event = russia2_russia.517
			}
		}
	}

	#No
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.516.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				add = -15
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM.FROM = {
					state = 268
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = russia2_russia.518
		}
	}
}

# FROM Accepts
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.517
	title = russia2_russia.517.t
	desc = russia2_russia.517.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
						state = 268
					}
				}
				goto_state = 268
				set_province_name = {
					id = 4985
					name = "New Moscow"
				}
				set_victory_points = {
					province = 4985
					value = 5
				}
				268 = {
					set_state_name = "Sagallo"
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
						state = 269
					}
				}
				269 = {
					set_state_name = "Russian Somaliland"
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Form a puppet
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.517.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.countries

				event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
					is_core_of = PREV
				}
				exists = no
			}
		}
		random_scope_in_array = {
			array = global.countries
			limit = {
				event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
					is_core_of = PREV
				}
				exists = no
			}
			
			transfer_state = event_target:sov_african_state_purchase
			ROOT = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_imperial_governorates
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 10
					neutrality = 70
					fascism = 10
					communism = 10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
							state = 268
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_template = "New Moscow Imperial Guard"
							}
						}
						set_technology = {
							tech_support = 1
							tech_engineers = 1
							gw_artillery = 1
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "New Moscow Imperial Guard"
							priority = 2
							regiments = {
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
								infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
								artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 2 }
								artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
							}
							support = {
								engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							}
						}
					}
					268 = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st New Moscow Imperial Guard Regiment\" division_template = \"New Moscow Imperial Guard\" start_experience_factor = 1.0 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
							owner = PREV
							prioritize_location = 4985
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"2nd New Moscow Imperial Guard Regiment\" division_template = \"New Moscow Imperial Guard\" start_experience_factor = 1.0 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
							owner = PREV
							prioritize_location = 4985
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Purchase_africa
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Purchase_africa
				days = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			modify_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Purchase_africa
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = russia2_russia.517.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		transfer_state = event_target:sov_african_state_purchase
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
						has_resistance = no
					}
				}
				event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
					start_resistance = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
				set_compliance = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Purchase_africa
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Purchase_africa
				days = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			modify_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Purchase_africa
				days = 30
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:sov_african_state_purchase = {
						state = 268
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_template = "New Moscow Imperial Guard"
						}
					}
					set_technology = {
						tech_support = 1
						tech_engineers = 1
						gw_artillery = 1
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "New Moscow Imperial Guard"
						priority = 2
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						}
						support = {
							engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				268 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"1st New Moscow Imperial Guard Regiment\" division_template = \"New Moscow Imperial Guard\" start_experience_factor = 1.0 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Give it to ally

			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {

#The Protestors Strikes Again
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.521
	title = russia2_russia.521.t
	desc = russia2_russia.521.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #We must stay vigilant
		name = russia2_russia.521.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = SOV
				is_core_of = SOV
				NOT = {
					state = 655
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				remove_state_core = PREV
			}
			PRT = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = protestors_destruction_variable
						value = 85
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					set_country_flag = killed_the_protestor_junta
					clr_country_flag = is_crushing_the_protestors
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = protestors_destruction_variable
					value = 10
				}
				randomize_variable = {
					var = protestors_destruction_variable
					distribution = uniform
					min = protestors_destruction_variable
					max = 100
				}
				round_variable = protestors_destruction_variable
			}
			SOV = {
				release = PRT
			}
			PRT = {
				add_ideas = SOV_Protestors_neutrality
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 20
					neutrality = 40
					fascism = 20
					communism = 20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PRT = {
							NOT = {
								has_template = "Protestors Division"
							}
						}
					}
					PRT = {
						division_template = {
							name = "Protestors Division"
							priority = 1

								infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }

								infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
								infantry = { x = 1 y = 4 }

								artillery_brigade = { x = 2 y = 1 }
							}
							support = {
								engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"1st Protestors Division\" division_template = \"Protestors Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = PRT
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"2nd Protestors Division\" division_template = \"Protestors Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = PRT
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"3rd Protestors Division\" division_template = \"Protestors Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = PRT
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"4th Protestors Division\" division_template = \"Protestors Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = PRT
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"5th Protestors Division\" division_template = \"Protestors Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = PRT
					}
					create_unit = {

#Fuck operations
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.523
	
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					controls_state = event_target:sov_target_country_revolution
				}
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.countries

					event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					exists = no
				}
			}
			random_scope_in_array = {
				array = global.countries
				limit = {
					event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					exists = no
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { revolution_normal_division_count = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { revolution_soviet_division_count = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
							has_resistance = yes
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { resistance_division_multiplier = event_target:sov_target_country_revolution.resistance }

					divide_temp_variable = { resistance_division_multiplier = 10 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
							}
						}
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 1
							max = 10
						}
					}
					else = {
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 1
							max = 5
						}
					}
					round_temp_variable = resistance_division_multiplier
					multiply_temp_variable = { revolution_normal_division_count = resistance_division_multiplier }

					divide_temp_variable = { resistance_division_multiplier = 2 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
							}
						}
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 1
							max = 10
						}
					}
					else = {
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 0
							max = 5
						}
					}
					round_temp_variable = resistance_division_multiplier
					multiply_temp_variable = { revolution_soviet_division_count = resistance_division_multiplier }
				}
				
				transfer_state = event_target:sov_target_country_revolution
				set_country_flag = liberated_by_sov
				leave_faction = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
						}
					}
					add_political_power = 300
					army_experience = 50
				}
				else = {
					add_political_power = 150
					army_experience = 25
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = liberator_workers }
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 0
						neutrality = 0
						fascism = 0
						communism = 100
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
					}
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = SOV_Fight_revolution
						days = 182
					}
					set_technology = {
						gw_artillery = 1
						tech_recon = 1
						tech_support = 1		
						tech_engineers = 1
					}

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_template = "Soviet Workers"
							}
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "Soviet Workers"
							priority = 1
							regiments = {
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
							}
							support = {
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								recon = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							}
						}
					}

					set_division_template_lock = {
						division_template = "Soviet Workers"
						is_locked = yes
					}

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_template = "Soviet Volunteers"
							}
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "Soviet Volunteers"
							priority = 2
							regiments = {
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
								artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 0 }
								artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							}
							support = {
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								recon = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								engineer = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							}
						}
					}

					set_division_template_lock = {
						division_template = "Soviet Volunteers"
						is_locked = yes
					}
					
					while_loop_effect = {
						break = break_loop
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								var = revolution_normal_division_count
								value = 1
								compare = greater_than_or_equals
							}
						}
						
						event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
							create_unit = {
								division = "name = \"Soviet Workers\" division_template = \"Soviet Workers\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
								owner = PREV
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = {
										var = revolution_soviet_division_count
										value = 1
										compare = greater_than_or_equals
									}
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Soviet Volunteers\" division_template = \"Soviet Volunteers\" start_experience_factor = 1"
									owner = PREV
								}
								PREV = {
									subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolution_soviet_division_count = 1 }
								}
							}
						}
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { revolution_normal_division_count = 1 }
					}

					ROOT = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = PREV
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { sov_trotsky_successful_revolution_count = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = sov_trotsky_successful_revolution_count
							value = 5
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						NOT = {
							is_in_array = { global.quick_revolution_achievement = THIS }
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { global.quick_revolution_achievement = THIS }
					set_variable = { global.quick_revolution_achievement_date@THIS = global.date }
					set_country_flag = russia_reworked_new_achievement
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_global_flag = russia_reworked_achievements_enabled
						}
						scoped_sound_effect = "russia_reworked_unlock_achievement"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = communism
						popularity = 0.1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				ROOT = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = communism
						popularity = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
						has_resistance = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
						}
					}
					event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
						add_resistance = 50
					}
				}
				else = {
					event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
						add_resistance = 25
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Really
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.524
	
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					controls_state = event_target:sov_target_country_revolution
				}
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.countries

					event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					exists = no
				}
			}
			random_scope_in_array = {
				array = global.countries
				limit = {
					event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					exists = no
				}

				set_temp_variable = { revolution_normal_division_count = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { revolution_soviet_division_count = 2 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:sov_target_country_revolution = {
							has_resistance = yes
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { resistance_division_multiplier = event_target:sov_target_country_revolution.resistance }

					divide_temp_variable = { resistance_division_multiplier = 10 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
							}
						}
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 1
							max = 10
						}
					}
					else = {
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 1
							max = 5
						}
					}
					round_temp_variable = resistance_division_multiplier
					multiply_temp_variable = { revolution_normal_division_count = resistance_division_multiplier }

					divide_temp_variable = { resistance_division_multiplier = 2 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
							}
						}
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 1
							max = 10
						}
					}
					else = {
						clamp_temp_variable = {
							var = resistance_division_multiplier
							min = 0
							max = 5
						}
					}
					round_temp_variable = resistance_division_multiplier
					multiply_temp_variable = { revolution_soviet_division_count = resistance_division_multiplier }
				}
				
				transfer_state = event_target:sov_target_country_revolution
				set_country_flag = liberated_by_sov
				leave_faction = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_completed_focus = SOV_liberation_of_the_workers
						}
					}
					add_political_power = 300
					army_experience = 50
				}
				else = {
					add_political_power = 150
					army_experience = 25
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = liberator_workers }
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 0
						neutrality = 0
						fascism = 0
						communism = 100
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
					}
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = SOV_Fight_revolution
						days = 182
					}
					set_technology = {
						gw_artillery = 1
						tech_recon = 1
						tech_support = 1		
						tech_engineers = 1
					}

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_template = "Soviet Workers"
							}
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "Soviet Workers"
							priority = 1
							regiments = {
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
							}
							support = {
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								recon = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							}
						}
					}

					set_division_template_lock = {
						division_template = "Soviet Workers"
						is_locked = yes
					}

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_template = "Soviet Volunteers"
							}
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "Soviet Volunteers"
							priority = 2
							regiments = {
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
								artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 0 }
								artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							}
							support = {
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								recon = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								engineer = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							}
						}

#Vote on Ultimatum
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.527
	title = russia2_russia.527.t
	desc = russia2_russia.527.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	timeout_days = 8

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Yes
		name = russia2_russia.527.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
			modifier = {
				add = -75
				OR = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = event_target:sov_current_democratic_target_event_target
						value > 50
					}
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = event_target:sov_current_democratic_target_event_target
					surrender_progress > 0.1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				OR = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = event_target:sov_current_democratic_target_event_target
						value > 25
					}
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = sov_voted_yes_last_vote
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_will_vote_for
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { current_democratic_vote^0 = 1 }
				add_to_array = { current_democratic_vote_for = THIS }
				add_to_array = { current_democratic_vote_registered = THIS }
				calculate_sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.527.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				OR = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = event_target:sov_current_democratic_target_event_target
						value > 50
					}
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = event_target:sov_current_democratic_target_event_target
					surrender_progress > 0.1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				OR = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = event_target:sov_current_democratic_target_event_target
						value > 25
					}
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = sov_voted_no_last_vote
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_will_vote_against
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				add_to_variable = { current_democratic_vote^1 = 1 }
				add_to_array = { current_democratic_vote_against = THIS }
				add_to_array = { current_democratic_vote_registered = THIS }
				calculate_sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Don't vote
		name = russia2_russia.527.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		set_country_flag = sov_voted_not_last_vote
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_will_skip_vote
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				add_to_array = { current_democratic_vote_not = THIS }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = russia2_russia.528
	title = russia2_russia.528.t
	desc = russia2_russia.528.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	timeout_days = 5
	
	option = { #Yay
		name = russia2_russia.528.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		clear_array = SOV.current_democratic_vote
		clear_array = SOV.current_democratic_vote_not
		clear_array = SOV.current_democratic_vote_for
		clear_array = SOV.current_democratic_vote_against
		clear_array = SOV.current_democratic_vote_registered
		clear_array = SOV.current_democratic_vote_participants
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = sov_democratic_target_alone
			}
			var:SOV.current_democratic_target = {
				country_event = russia2_russia.533
			}
			clr_country_flag = sov_democratic_target_alone
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = sov_democratic_target_alliance
			}
			var:SOV.current_democratic_target = {
				country_event = russia2_russia.530
			}
			clr_country_flag = sov_democratic_target_alliance
		}
		clr_country_flag = sov_democratic_vote_started
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_democratic_can_launch_another_vote
	}
}

#Democratic Russia Demands Dismantle of our Faction
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.530
	title = russia2_russia.530.t
	desc = russia2_russia.530.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Yes
		name = russia2_russia.530.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				any_country = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					is_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				num_faction_members > 10
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 0.25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_subject = no
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_Restrictions_democratic_russia
			days = 90
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.531 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.530.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				any_country = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					is_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				num_faction_members > 10
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 0.25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = will_lead_to_war_with_sov_democratic
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.532 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = russia2_russia.539.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Accept
		name = russia2_russia.539.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_state = {
					is_claimed_by = SOV
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_government = democratic
				OR = {
					is_guaranteed_by = SOV
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = SOV
					has_opinion = {
						target = SOV
						value > 49
					}
					has_country_flag = sov_friendship_treaty_signed
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -35
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_major = yes
					num_faction_members > 10
					has_opinion = {
						target = SOV
						value < -50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT					
					}
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				FROM = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = SOV
			value = 500
		}
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.540 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = russia2_russia.539.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				add = 65
				any_state = {
					is_claimed_by = SOV
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25

					has_opinion = {
						target = SOV
						value > 49
					}
					has_country_flag = sov_friendship_treaty_signed
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 35
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_major = yes
					num_faction_members > 10
					has_opinion = {
						target = SOV
						value < -50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = sov_friendship_treaty_signed
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		FROM = {

country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.546
	title = russia2_russia.546.t
	desc = russia2_russia.546.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Yes
		name = russia2_russia.546.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = accepted_faction_join_democratic_sov
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.547 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { investment_level = SOV.russian_investment@ROOT }
			set_temp_variable = { min_days = 182 }
			set_temp_variable = { max_days = 365 }
			set_temp_variable = { days_event = 60 }
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = investment_level
						value = 1
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { min_days = 60 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { max_days = 60 }
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = min_days
					min = 30
					max = 182
				}
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = max_days
					min = 60
					max = 365
				}
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { investment_level = 1 }
			}
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = days_event
				distribution = uniform
				min = var:min_days
				max = var:max_days
			}
			round_temp_variable = days_event
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.549 days = var:days_event }
		}	
	}

	option = { #No
		name = russia2_russia.546.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = refused_faction_join_democratic_sov
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.548 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

	id = russia2_russia.551
	title = russia2_russia.551.t
	desc = russia2_russia.551.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Oops
		name = russia2_russia.551.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_europe
						has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_asia
						has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_caucasus
					}
					has_country_flag = is_russian_state_faction_leader_democratic
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_europe
						has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_asia
						has_country_flag = democratic_russia_chaos_caucasus
					}
					has_country_flag = is_russian_state_faction_leader_democratic
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_faction = anti_russian_coalition
			set_country_flag = is_russian_state_faction_leader_democratic
		}
		set_country_flag = russian_state_extreme_ideology
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_democratic_russia_will_attack_soon
	}
}

#START OF PURGE EVENTS
#Mikhail Tukhachevsky
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.554
	title = russia2_russia.554.t
	desc = russia2_russia.554.d

	picture = GFX_0_Mikhail_tukhachevsky_purge_event

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_government = communism
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = mikhail_tukhachevsky_purge
			has_completed_focus = SOV_great_purge2
		}
		focus_progress = {
			focus = SOV_great_purge2
			progress > 0.25
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = mikhail_tukhachevsky_purge
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	
	option = { #Purge
		name = russia2_russia.554.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		set_country_flag = mikhail_tukhachevsky_purged
		set_variable = { sov_great_purge_frame^0 = 2 }
		set_variable = { sov_great_purge_date^0 = global.date }
		add_to_variable = { sov_great_purge_completion = 10 }
		round_variable = sov_great_purge_completion
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sov_great_purge_completion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_add_10_purge_completion
		sov_increase_great_purge_penalties = yes
		remove_unit_leader = 401
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_theorist
		show_ideas_tooltip = SOV_Mikhail_tukhachevsky
	}

	option = { #Don't purge
		name = russia2_russia.554.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_remove_5_purge_completion
		set_country_flag = mikhail_tukhachevsky_not_purged
		add_political_power = -100
		subtract_from_variable = { sov_great_purge_completion = 5 }
		round_variable = sov_great_purge_completion
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sov_great_purge_completion

#Georgy Zhukov
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.555
	title = russia2_russia.555.t
	desc = russia2_russia.555.d

	picture = GFX_1_Georgy_zhukov_purge_event

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_government = communism
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = georgy_zhukov_purge
			has_completed_focus = SOV_great_purge2
		}
		focus_progress = {
			focus = SOV_great_purge2
			progress > 0.5
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = georgy_zhukov_purge
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	
	option = { #Purge
		name = russia2_russia.555.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		set_country_flag = georgy_zhukov_purged
		set_variable = { sov_great_purge_frame^1 = 2 }
		set_variable = { sov_great_purge_date^1 = global.date }
		add_to_variable = { sov_great_purge_completion = 10 }
		round_variable = sov_great_purge_completion
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sov_great_purge_completion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_add_10_purge_completion
		sov_increase_great_purge_penalties = yes
		remove_unit_leader = 410
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_theorist
		show_ideas_tooltip = SOV_Georgy_zhukov
	}

	option = { #Don't purge
		name = russia2_russia.555.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_remove_5_purge_completion
		set_country_flag = georgy_zhukov_not_purged
		add_political_power = -100
		subtract_from_variable = { sov_great_purge_completion = 5 }
		round_variable = sov_great_purge_completion
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sov_great_purge_completion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_remove_1_purge_completion
		add_political_power = -50
		subtract_from_variable = { sov_great_purge_completion = 1 }
		round_variable = sov_great_purge_completion
		clamp_variable = {
			var = sov_great_purge_completion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
	}
}

		has_global_flag = second_russian_civil_war_in_progress

		has_government = communism
		has_war = no

			is_neighbor_of = TAN
		}

			exists = yes

			is_subject = no
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}

#Assassinate FROM leader
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.615
	title = russia2_russia.615.t
	desc = russia2_russia.615.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:SOV_replace_from_leader_event_target = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = sov_correct_assassination_attempts^num
						value = 0
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
				clear_array = sov_correct_assassination_attempts
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				break = end_array
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = sov_correct_assassination_attempts^num
						value = 2
						compare = less_than
					}
				}

				set_temp_variable = { get_random_option = 0 }
				randomize_temp_variable = {
					var = get_random_option
					distribution = uniform
					min = 1
					max = 5
				}
				round_temp_variable = get_random_option
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = get_random_option
							value = 5
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { get_random_option = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_in_array = { sov_correct_assassination_attempts = get_random_option }
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { sov_correct_assassination_attempts = get_random_option }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Use poison
		name = russia2_russia.615.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:SOV_replace_from_leader_event_target = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { sov_correct_assassination_attempts = 1 }
					}
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.616 days = 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.617 days = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.618 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Hire a hitman
		name = russia2_russia.615.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:SOV_replace_from_leader_event_target = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { sov_correct_assassination_attempts = 2 }
					}
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.616 days = 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.617 days = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.618 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Plant a bomb in their car
		name = russia2_russia.615.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:SOV_replace_from_leader_event_target = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { sov_correct_assassination_attempts = 3 }
					}
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.616 days = 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.617 days = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.618 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Political scandal
		name = russia2_russia.615.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:SOV_replace_from_leader_event_target = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { sov_correct_assassination_attempts = 4 }
					}
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.616 days = 1 }
					}
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.617 days = 1 }
				}
				else = {
					ROOT = {
						country_event = { id = russia2_russia.618 days = 1 }
					}
				}
