#Leader Assassinated!
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.617
	title = russia2_russia.617.t
	desc = russia2_russia.617.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_ruins

	is_triggered_only = yes

	timeout_days = 5

	option = { #What?!
		name = russia2_russia.617.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = leader_dies_from_sov
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_country_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					kill_ideology_leader = communism
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							communism < 0.5
						}
						set_political_party = {
							ideology = communism
							popularity = 50
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = communism
							popularity = 0.1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = communism
						popularity = 0.1
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = soviet_puppet
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							tag = MAN
							tag = MEN
							tag = SHX
							tag = PRC
							tag = XSM
							tag = SIK
							tag = YUN
							tag = GXC
							is_literally_china = yes
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_leader_with_trait = making_fun_of_me_uh
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_trait = making_fun_of_me_uh
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = no
							NOT = {
								is_in_array = { global.making_fun_of_me_uh_achievement = THIS }
							}
						}
						add_to_array = { global.making_fun_of_me_uh_achievement = THIS }
						set_variable = { global.making_fun_of_me_uh_achievement_date@THIS = global.date }
						set_country_flag = russia_reworked_new_achievement
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_global_flag = russia_reworked_achievements_enabled
							}
							scoped_sound_effect = "russia_reworked_unlock_achievement"
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
					}
					kill_ideology_leader = democratic
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							democratic < 0.5
						}
						set_political_party = {
							ideology = democratic
							popularity = 50
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = democratic
							popularity = 0.1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_elections = yes
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = democratic
							elections_allowed = no
						}
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.1
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = russian_puppet
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Member_of_the_league_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Member_of_the_league_idea
					add_idea = SOV_Member_of_the_league_idea_2
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_Head_of_the_league_idea
				add_idea = SOV_Head_of_the_league_idea_2
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.620 days = 5 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = every_members_of_the_league_gain_military_bonus
	}

	option = { #Internal Stability
		name = russia2_russia.619.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.620 days = 5 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Member_of_the_league_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Member_of_the_league_idea
					add_idea = SOV_Member_of_the_league_idea_3
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_Head_of_the_league_idea
				add_idea = SOV_Head_of_the_league_idea_3
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = every_members_of_the_league_gain_politics_bonus
	}

#State of our Neutrality
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.625
	title = russia2_russia.625.t
	desc = russia2_russia.625.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bul_troops_macedonia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Join Ennemy
		name = russia2_russia.625.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = reunification_war_is_ongoing_anarchist
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = is_neutral_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
		set_country_flag = is_ennemy_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
		add_to_array = { global.sov_ancient_federation_member_who_left_the_league = ROOT }
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.626 }
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.sov_ancient_federation_member_who_left_the_league
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = SOV
					}
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						TAG = SOV
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
						has_country_flag = is_friend_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.sov_ancient_federation_member_who_left_the_league
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						TAG = SOV
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = SOV
						}
						has_country_flag = is_ennemy_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
					}
					give_military_access = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Join SOV
		name = russia2_russia.625.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			has_global_flag = reunification_war_is_ongoing_anarchist
		}
		clr_country_flag = is_neutral_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
		set_country_flag = is_friend_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
		SOV = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.627 }
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.sov_ancient_federation_member_who_left_the_league
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						TAG = SOV
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Neutrality
		name = russia2_russia.625.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = reunification_war_is_ongoing_anarchist
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.628 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Nothing
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = reunification_war_is_ongoing_anarchist
			}
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		name = russia2_russia.625.d
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#Randomise Opinion of Russian Reunification
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.630
	title = russia2_russia.630.t
	desc = russia2_russia.630.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_temp_variable = { opinion_russian_anarchist_var_temp = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = opinion_russian_anarchist_var_temp
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { opinion_russian_anarchist_var_temp = 100 }
		round_temp_variable = opinion_russian_anarchist_var_temp
		set_variable = { opinion_russian_anarchist_var_true = opinion_russian_anarchist_var_temp }
	}

	option = { #Results
		name = russia2_russia.630.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = opinion_russian_anarchist_var_true
					value = 45
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = russia2_russia.621 }
			set_country_flag = is_ennemy_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
			add_to_array = { global.sov_ancient_federation_member_who_left_the_league = THIS }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = opinion_russian_anarchist_var_true
					value = 65
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = is_friend_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = is_neutral_of_anarchist_russia_league_edition
		}
	}
}

#Randomise Opinion of Russian Reunification
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.638
	title = russia2_russia.630.t
	desc = russia2_russia.630.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { opinion_russian_anarchist_puppet_reform_plan = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = opinion_russian_anarchist_puppet_reform_plan
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { opinion_russian_anarchist_puppet_reform_plan = 100 }
		round_temp_variable = opinion_russian_anarchist_puppet_reform_plan
		set_variable = { personality_russian_anarchist_indicator = 0 }
		randomize_temp_variable = { #1 is militaristic(like 2, hate 4), 2 is economic(like 1, hate 3), 3 is social(like 4, hate 2), last is peaceful (like 3, hate 1)
			var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
			distribution = uniform
			min = 0
			max = 4
		}
		round_temp_variable = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
	}

	option = { #Results
		name = russia2_russia.630.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
					value = 1
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_variable = { militaristic_personality_type_anarchist = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
					value = 2
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_variable = { economic_personality_type_anarchist = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
					value = 2
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
					value = 3
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_variable = { social_personality_type_anarchist = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
					value = 3
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = personality_russian_anarchist_indicator
					value = 4
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_variable = { peaceful_personality_type_anarchist = 0 }
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				country_event = { id = russia2_russia.643 days = 4 }

		}
		else_if = {

#Hidden Event For Event Generator
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.642

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			33 = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.639 }
					set_country_flag = meeting_with_from_leader_loc
				}
			}
			33 = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.640 }
					set_country_flag = public_speech_citizens_loc
				}
			}
			33 = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = russia2_russia.641 }
					set_country_flag = public_speech_workers_loc
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Choice was Excelent
country_event = {
	id = russia2_russia.643
	title = russia2_russia.643.t
	desc = {
		text = russia2_russia.643.d_1
		trigger = {
			SOV = {
				has_country_flag = meeting_with_from_leader_loc
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = russia2_russia.643.d_2
		trigger = {
			SOV = {
				has_country_flag = public_speech_citizens_loc
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = russia2_russia.643.d_3
		trigger = {
			SOV = {
				has_country_flag = public_speech_workers_loc
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_handshake_russia2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Excelent
		name = russia2_russia.643.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = from_will_receiv_20_points_project_anarchist
		FROM = {
			add_to_variable = { opinion_russian_anarchist_puppet_reform_plan = 20 }
		}
		clr_country_flag = meeting_with_from_leader_loc
		clr_country_flag = public_speech_citizens_loc
		clr_country_flag = public_speech_workers_loc
	}
}
